## <a id="prompt-2001734583830626600">å¤å¤ç…§ç›¸äº­é‡Œçš„ç”œèœœç¬é—´</a> (<a href="https://twitter.com/miilesus/status/2001734583830626635" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Melisâœ¨</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-18/2001734583830626600_1.jpg" alt="å¤å¤ç…§ç›¸äº­é‡Œçš„ç”œèœœç¬é—´">

```
Create a realistic vintage-style photo booth / Polaroid photo collage featuring the same couple, using the two uploaded images as exact face references for both individuals (preserve both identities accurately).
The couple appears natural, affectionate, and playful, captured in multiple candid moments as if taken inside a photo booth. The woman and the man maintain their original facial features, skin tones, and expressions.
Woman: elegant, feminine, glowing skin, natural makeup, soft blush, glossy lips, long dark hair styled loosely with gentle volume. Wearing a minimal strapless cream or light beige dress.
Man: clean and handsome appearance, short dark hair, light stubble or clean-shaven, wearing a black leather jacket over a white shirt
Scenes & poses included in the collage:
The woman smiling brightly while the man stands behind her playfully covering her eyes.
The couple standing close, facing each other lovingly, her hand resting on his chest.
A close face-to-face moment with soft smiles and eye contact.
The woman standing behind the man, making a peace sign while smiling at the camera.
A playful dancing pose where the man lifts one of the womanâ€™s hands as if spinning her.
A relaxed, candid moment where both laugh naturally at the camera.
Environment: neutral photo booth backdrop with soft vertical curtains, warm indoor lighting, subtle shadows, cozy and intimate atmosphere.
Photography style: vintage Polaroid / analog photo booth aesthetic, slightly soft focus, gentle grain, mild blur, natural imperfections, warm tones, realistic skin texture.
Lighting: soft frontal flash combined with ambient light, creating a casual, real-life snapshot feeling.
Mood & vibe: romantic, playful, spontaneous, intimate, youthful, nostalgic.
Composition: multi-frame vertical collage, evenly spaced images, authentic photo booth layout.
Quality: high realism, not AI-looking, natural proportions, no distortion.
```

```

- å¥³æ€§ç«™åœ¨ç”·æ€§èº«åï¼Œå¯¹ç€é•œå¤´æ¯”å‡ºå’Œå¹³æ‰‹åŠ¿å¹¶å¾®ç¬‘ã€‚

Keep product recognition and professional quality consistent, but make each cell visually distinct.

## <a id="prompt-2001258985358606600">å…‰å½±äºŒç»´ç ï¼šæ‰‹ä¸å…‰çš„ç²¾å¯†åä½œ</a> (<a href="https://x.com/Gorden_Sun/status/2001258985358606605" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Gorden Sun</a>)

## <a id="prompt-2001337146905690600">åˆ†å±å †å ï¼š1Ã—4æ„å›¾æ³•</a> (<a href="https://x.com/henrydaubrez/status/2001337146905690519" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Henry Daubrez ğŸŒ¸ğŸ’€</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-17/2001337146905690600_0.jpg" alt="åˆ†å±å †å ï¼š1Ã—4æ„å›¾æ³•">

```
SPLIT STACK (1X4 grid)

Now that everyone has gotten the 3x3 grids out of their system for generating different angles, it feels like the right moment to double down on something I shared on day one of Nano Bananaâ€™s public release.

You will get more consistent results using a vertical image split into four frames (what I call a split stack), then splitting and extracting from there.

Lost detail is lost.

A 3x3 grid can give you something decent, but consistency quickly breaks down. Angles drift. Details soften. The model starts inventing what it thinks you want because its attention is split across 9, 12, or 16 frames at once.

Personally, I use 1x4 vertical grids and export each frame to 16:9 afterward.

Two reasons:
1/ It preserves detail and consistency shot after shot.
Instead of playing roulette by asking for random angles, it forces you to be intentional. 
2/You describe the shot you need, the background you expect, and the framing that serves your story. Nano Banana Pro still struggles with environment rotation unless you guide it very explicitly.

You do you. But I have watched the 3x3 approach go viral a week after this method was shared, get adopted by everyone, and now I am seeing many of those same people quietly move away from it because it does not deliver on consistency.

Trends move fast. Fundamentals still matter.
```

```

on  Photorealistic ultra-wide desert scene in Egypt near the Giza plateau at golden hour. A colossal inverted pyramid, point-down, dominates the landscape at an unimaginable scale, dwarfing the horizon. Its vast upper rim stretches for multiple kilometers, while the sloping faces plunge inward toward a needle-like apex that hovers just above the sand, leaving a gigantic shadowed void beneath. The surface reads as ancient limestone blocks with dark granite inlays: mega-sized courses, eroded edges, wind-sanded wear, and long, faint bands of hieroglyphs that only appear where the sun grazes the stone. Include tiny scale cues in the distance: a thin line of tourists like ants, a few small buses and 4x4s parked far away, a camel caravan crossing the flats, and scattered survey flags. Heat haze and dust plumes soften the far edges. Sand dunes climb the lower planes where stone meets desert, with drifting sand spilling down seams like a slow waterfall. Pale sky, low sun, strong raking light, extreme HDR realism, crisp micro-textures, natural color grading, no glow or energy effects.
```

```

## <a id="prompt-2000884207028179500">Luxury Product Grid Campaign</a> (<a href="https://x.com/azed_ai/status/2000884207028179418?s=20" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Amira Zairi</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-16/2000884207028179500_0.jpg" alt="Luxury Product Grid Campaign">

```
Create a 3Ã—3 grid in
3:4 aspect ratio for a high-end commercial marketing campaign using the uploaded product as the central subject.

Each frame must present a distinct visual concept while maintaining perfect product consistency across all nine images.

Grid Concepts (one per cell):

1. Iconic hero still life with bold composition

2. Extreme macro detail highlighting material, surface, or texture

3. Dynamic liquid or particle interaction surrounding the product

4. Minimal sculptural arrangement with abstract forms

5. Floating elements composition suggesting lightness and innovation

6. Sensory close-up emphasizing tactility and realism

7. Color-driven conceptual scene inspired by the product palette

8. Ingredient or component abstraction (non-literal, symbolic)

9. Surreal yet elegant fusion scene combining realism and imagination

Visual Rules:
Product must remain 100% accurate in shape, proportions, label, typography, color, and branding
No distortion, deformation, or redesign of the product
Clean separation between product and background

Lighting & Style:
Soft, controlled studio lighting
Subtle highlights, realistic shadows
High dynamic range, ultra-sharp focus
Editorial luxury advertising aesthetic
Premium sensory marketing look

Overall Feel:
Modern, refined, visually cohesive
High-end commercial campaign
Designed for brand websites, social grids, and digital billboards
Hyperreal, cinematic, polished, and aspirational
```

## <a id="prompt-2000711160736227600">Nedçš„èµ›åšæœ‹å…‹å¤œè¡Œ</a> (<a href="https://x.com/GenoQuest/status/2000711160736227576" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Geno</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-15/2000711160736227600_0.jpg" alt="Nedçš„èµ›åšæœ‹å…‹å¤œè¡Œ">

```
Is multi-image storytelling grids possible for Grok Imagine? It seems so. I got inspired by the Nano Banana pro+Claude posts ive been seeing of this trend. Tried this with Grok, about a pixar like style telling the story of Ned, cyberpunk setting, he walks through the city. Deets:

A single cohesive image divided into a clean 3x3 grid with thin white borders, telling a sequential story of a young Pixar-style cyberpunk protagonist named Ned traveling through a bustling futuristic city at night. Character consistency: Ned is a teenage boy with messy brown hair, large expressive green eyes, freckles, wearing a worn oversized hoodie with glowing circuit patterns, cargo pants, and sneakers, with the same exact appearance in every panel. Style: Highly detailed Pixar/Disney animation style, smooth CGI rendering, vibrant saturated colors, dramatic cinematic lighting with neon blues, pinks, and purples reflecting on wet surfaces, subtle lens flares, volumetric god rays from holograms and headlights. Grid layout and story progression (top left to bottom right, reading order): 1. Wide establishing shot: Ned standing on a rainy rooftop overlooking the massive cyberpunk city skyline filled with towering skyscrapers, flying cars, giant holographic billboards, and neon signs. 2. Medium shot: Ned leaping from rooftop to rooftop, cape-like hoodie flapping in the wind, determined expression. 3. Close-up: Ned landing on a lower platform, looking curious at a glowing street food vendor drone hovering nearby. 4. Wide shot: Ned walking through a crowded neon-lit street market, people and aliens around him, steam rising from food stalls, rain falling. 5. Medium shot: Ned stopping to watch a massive holographic advertisement of a futuristic band performing in mid-air. 6. Action shot: Ned running through an alley as police drones fly overhead, dramatic low-angle view. 7. Close-up: Ned's face in profile, reflective and thoughtful, city lights reflecting in his eyes. 8. Medium shot: Ned climbing a fire escape ladder toward a higher platform. 9. Final wide shot: Ned reaching the top, standing triumphantly with arms outstretched, the entire sprawling cyberpunk city glowing below him under a stormy sky. Aspect ratio 16:9, ultra-detailed, masterpiece, best quality.
```

## <a id="prompt-2000394883056710100">Neon Monument: Futuristic Brand Facade</a> (<a href="https://x.com/berryxia/status/2000394883056710091" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Berryxia.AI</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-15/2000394883056710100_0.jpg" alt="Neon Monument: Futuristic Brand Facade">

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-15/2000394883056710100_1.jpg" alt="Neon Monument: Futuristic Brand Facade">

```
A perfectly, mathematically straight-on, direct frontal architectural photograph taken precisely at eye-level at night. The composition is an orthographic view, with zero perspective distortion, presenting the scene as a perfectly flat geometric elevation. 
It captures a monumental, highly sculptural 3D neon commercial sign mounted dead center on a futuristic \"smart\" building facade. 
The facade is composed of textured dark metallic cladding with visible weathering (oxidized patina, rain streaks), integrated with subtle, slow-pulsing [ADAPTIVE_TONE] architectural LED accent strips that complement the sign's color temperature.

// 1. BRAND NAME SECTION (Intelligent Scaling)

The brand name section at the top features the **complete and full sequence** of the large Chinese characters \"[INPUT_BRAND_NAME]\". **All characters provided must be clearly rendered without any truncation or abbreviation.** They are arranged horizontally across the upper section, constructed as **deep, extruded metal channel letters** (depth: [AUTO_DEPTH]cm based on name length) housing **[AUTO_LAYER_COUNT] stacked layers of exposed glass neon tubes**. These tubes glow in [INPUT_BRAND_COLOR], encased behind thick, clear textured acrylic plates (visible micro-scratches, slight frosting) that create complex light refractions, chromatic aberration at edges, and immense depth viewed directly from the front. Character spacing: [AUTO_KERNING] for optimal readability.

// 2. LOGO EMBLEM (Dynamic Sizing)

To the right is a **protruding, dimensional emblem logo** (size: [AUTO_LOGO_SIZE] relative to brand name length) incorporating \"[INPUT_LOGO_DESCRIPTION]\". It features [INPUT_LOGO_COLOR] neon outlines with backlighting that makes it float off the background surface. Logo mounting includes visible polished chrome stand-offs with bolt details.

// 3. CATEGORY TEXT (Smart Line Breaking)

Directly below, the category text \"[INPUT_CATEGORY_NAME]\" is rendered in **thick, stacked layers of [INPUT_CATEGORY_COLOR] neon tubes** set deep within raw, brushed metal channels (visible weld seams). If category text exceeds 6 characters, it automatically splits into two lines with balanced character distribution. Provides strong, heavy industrial contrast with [AUTO_CONTRAST_LEVEL] intensity.

// 4. ENGLISH/TAGLINE (Floating Typography)

At the bottom, the English text \"[INPUT_ENGLISH_TEXT]\" is in smaller **single-line [INPUT_ACCENT_COLOR] neon tubes** mounted on a raised transparent acrylic support bar (8mm thickness, visible edge lighting), giving a floating appearance. Font weight adjusts to [AUTO_WEIGHT] based on text length.

// 5. ADVANCED MATERIAL DETAILS

The entire structure emphasizes heavy industrial 3D construction with realistic weathering:
- **Metal Framework:** Visible thick steel framing with oxidized copper patina, exposed bolt heads (M12 hex), TIG weld seams with slight discoloration
- **Chrome Stand-offs:** Polished mirror-finish mounting hardware with Fresnel reflections and subtle fingerprint smudges
- **Wiring Conduits:** Exposed flexible metal conduits with cable strain relief clamps, proper bend radius
- **Acrylic Enclosures:** 12mm thick cast acrylic with UV yellowing simulation, micro-scratches from maintenance, slight warping from heat
- **Neon Tubes:** Borosilicate glass tubes (15mm diameter) with electrode glow at ends, slight gas color shift indicating age (argon blue aging to subtle purple tint)

// 6. ENHANCED LIGHTING PHYSICS

The intense multi-colored glow interacts with the environment through advanced light physics:
- **Volumetric Scattering:** Atmospheric haze with Rayleigh scattering (blue light scatter) and Mie scattering (larger particle glow)
- **HDR Bloom:** Physically accurate bloom with inverse-square falloff, creating star-burst effects on brightest neon sections
- **Chromatic Aberration:** Slight RGB color separation visible at high-contrast edges of neon tubes
- **Fresnel Reflections:** Angle-dependent specular highlights on chrome hardware and wet metallic facade
- **Caustics:** Complex light patterns from textured acrylic refracting onto metallic cladding
- **Ambient Occlusion:** Contact shadows where sign mounts to facade, enhancing depth perception
- **Light Bleed:** [INPUT_BRAND_COLOR] light spilling onto adjacent LED strips, creating color temperature mixing zones
- **Rain Effect (Optional):** Water droplets on facade creating lens effect, light streaks, and enhanced reflections

// 7. ATMOSPHERIC CONTEXT

The atmosphere is bustling urban technological at night with:
- Distant city glow creating ambient light pollution (warm orange sky gradient)
- Subtle steam/mist rising from street level
- Lens flare from brightest neon elements
- Sharp specular highlights across architectural surface
- [AUTO_WEATHER_MOOD]: Clear/Misty/Light Rain based on brand personality

// 8. TECHNICAL SPECIFICATIONS

- **Resolution:** 8K (7680Ã—4320) for maximum detail
- **Color Space:** Wide-gamut HDR (Rec. 2020)
- **Camera Simulation:** Hasselblad H6D-400c MS, 80mm lens, f/11, ISO 400, 2-second exposure
- **Lighting Setup:** Ambient night exposure + neon practical lighting
- **Post-Processing:** Minimal color grading to preserve neon color accuracy
- **Aspect Ratio:** ã€9:16 (vertical/portrait orientation) ã€‘
```

```
[PERSON] , presented as a direct uncompressed digital screen export of a flat source graphic file.

Technical & Composition Rules:

Medium (Crucial): This is native digital pixel art, NOT a photograph. The entire canvas from edge to edge is pure, seamless digital white (RGB 255,255,255). There is ZERO physical reality: no paper grain, no ink texture, no frame, no shadows, no lighting gradients, no desk/wall environment. It is a flat 2D digital rendering meant for screen display only.

The color must be uniquely distinct and semantically relevant to the subject (e.g., David Beckham = classic England white/red or Man Utd red; Prince = Purple). Avoid defaulting to generic red unless justified by primary branding.

Subject Element: A high-detail, gritty black-and-white photograph of the subject is digitally masked inside and over the colored rectangle container. The subject is cropped from the chest up, preferably in a side profile or dynamic 3/4 angle. The head slightly overlaps the top edge of the colored container.

Typography (Digital Text Elements):

Last Name: Placed below the colored container in the white digital space. Rendered in a tall, compressed, bold sans-serif digital font. Color matches the container.

First Name (Contrast Rule): Layered over the subject's torso/clothing. Rendered in a loose, handwritten "signature" script style. The color matches the container, BUT it must be perfectly legible. Ensure high contrast against the underlying B&W photo pixels.

No text covers the face.

Header Element: Centered at the very top in the white digital space, place a small, iconic logo strictly associated with the subject (or their clean uppercase initials if no logo exists), matched to the container's color.

## <a id="prompt-2000883616989974800">Nano Banana Proï¼šå»ºç­‘çµæ„Ÿæ™ºèƒ½å°å·¥å…·</a> (<a href="https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2000883616989974693" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Gadgetify</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-16/2000883616989974800_0.jpg" alt="Nano Banana Proï¼šå»ºç­‘çµæ„Ÿæ™ºèƒ½å°å·¥å…·">

```
Step 1: Select 3 famous architectural landmarks of a random country
Step 2: Deeply analyze geometry, structural principles, material appearances, proportions, and symbolic features.
Step 3: Scale concepts down dramatically and fuse elements into 9 distinct everyday high-tech home or personal devices (kitchen, desk, wellness, garden).
Step 4: Ensure each invention solves a real 2025 consumer pain point with smart features (app control, sustainability, modularity).
Step 5: Produce a 3x3 grid of premium product photography on relevant surfaces (marble counter, oak desk), shallow DOF, luxurious lighting, catchy inventive names underneath. Include subtle UI glows or motion hints for functionality. include names
```
